## Diagram 2

```mermaid
classDiagram
  class Project {
    +string name = "core"
    +string version = "0.1.0"
    +string description = "FreightVerify Shared Core Library"
    +string readme = "README.md"
    +string requires_python = ">=3.13"
  }
  class BuildSystem {
    +string backend = "setuptools.build_meta"
    +list requires = ["setuptools>=61.0"]
  }
  class PackageDiscovery {
    +where = ["src"]
    +include = ["core*"]
  }
  class Dependencies {
    +runtime = ["pydantic>=2.0","pydantic-settings>=2.0","SQLAlchemy>=2.0","boto3>=1.34","psycopg[binary]>=3.2"]
    +optional.dev = ["pytest","ruff","pyright","httpx"]
  }
  Project <-- BuildSystem
  Project <-- PackageDiscovery
  Project <-- Dependencies
```
